(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)) (not (closed ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?sharp_o) (holding ?co))

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)) (not (closed ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?sharp_o) (holding ?co))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)) (not (closed ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?sharp_o) (holding ?co))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)) (not (closed ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?sharp_o) (holding ?co))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)) (not (closed ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?sharp_o) (holding ?co))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?sharp_o) (holding ?co))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

    :parameters (?o - object)

    :effect (used ?o)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?sharp_o) (holding ?co))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contains ?r ?sharp_o) (holding ?co))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )

  )

  )

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))

  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :equality :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (not (used ?o)))
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
)
